MAC0001-A.
Title: Vision of Theophilus of Alexandria.
Text: Budge, Miracles, p. 62; TGS-101, p. 337.
Summary:
English translation:
PEth: 41.8 (21r-30r); 41.80 (110v-113r); 41.81 (113r-115v);
EMIP: 601.225 (139r–143v); 601.358 (190v–191v); 601.351 (187r–188r);
MSS: G-1; BM 2-39; VLVE 298 (124r).
EMML: 6938 (9r); 7543 (7r); 3051 (67v); 2058 (16r); 3031(81v); 2424 (52r); 642 (13v).
Keywords: Egypt; Flight into Egypt; Visions, apparitions; Holy Family; Families; Patriarchs (ecclesiastical); Theophilus, Patriarch of Alexandria;
Incipit: Ba-ʾǝnta za-kama ʾastārʾayatto la-Tewofǝlos, liqa ṗāṗṗāsāt, wa-za-kama, tanāgaratto wa-ʾaṣnāʿatto ʾǝm-dakāma fǝnot. Yǝbe Tewofǝlos liqa ṗāṗṗāsāt: Sǝmʿu, ʾabawǝya wa-ʾaḫawǝya, za-ʾenaggǝrakkǝmu ba-ferhāt wa-ba-raʿād wa-ba­hāymānot rǝtǝʿt (6938) /
Fid-Incipit: በእንተ፡ ዘከመ፡ አስተርአየቶ፡ ለቴዎፍሎስ፡ ሊቀ፡ ጳጳሳት፡ ስምዑ፡ አበውየ፡ ወአኀውየ፡ ዘእነግረክሙ፡ በፍርሃት፡ ወበረዓድ፡ ወበሃይማኖት፡ ርትዕት፡.
Note: Parts of this miracle can occur as distinct miracles (see below).


MAC0001-B.
Title: Vision of Theophilus of Alexandria (continued): Satan appears to King Herod and advises him to kill the Innocents.
Text: T-101, p. 343:77.
PEth:
MSS: None.
EMML: 1606 (54v).
Keywords: Herod, King of Israel; Innocents; Priests; Satan; Simeon, Jewish priest; Magi; Patriarchs (ecclesiastical); Theophilus, Patriarch of Alexandria;
Incipit: wa-ba-yeʾeti ʿǝlat mota Sǝmʿon kāhǝn ʾaragāwi. Wa-nabara Herods 2 ʿāmata ʾǝnza yǝṣannǝḥomu la-sabʾa sagal (1606) / ወበይእቲ፡ ዕለት፡ ሞተ፡ ስምዖን፡ ካህን፡ አረጋዊ። ወነበረ፡ ሄሮድስ፡ ፪ዓመተ፡ እንዘ፡ ይጸንሖሙ፡ ለሰብአ፡ ሰገል፡.


MAC0001-C.
Title: Vision of Theophilus of Alexandria (continued): The arrival of the Holy Family in Sāmǝnon.
Text: T-101, p. 347:118.
PEth:
MSS: None.
EMML: 1156 (106r); 1606 (55r).
Keywords: Egypt; Flight into Egypt; Holy Family; Families; Sāmǝnon; Patriarchs (ecclesiastical); Samenon; Temples (pagan); Theophilus, Patriarch of Alexandria; Towers;
Incipit: Wa-ʾǝm-zǝ baṣḥa hagara Sāmǝnon; wǝsta qadāmi ʾanqaṣ māḫfad ba-4 māʿzǝnihu, wa-yǝtleʿāl ʾǝmkwǝllu hagar (1606) / ወእምዝ፡ በጽሐ፡ ሀገረ፡ ሳምኖን፡ ውስተ፡ ቀዳሚ፡ አንቀጽ፡ ማኅፈድ፡ በ፬ማዕዝኒሁ፡ ወይትሌዓል፡ እምኵሉ፡ ሀገር፡.

Incipit: Ba-ʾǝnta za-kama ʾastarʾayatto la-Tewofǝlos… ʾǝm-dǝkāma fǝnot… Wa-ʾǝnza kama-zǝ, ʾastarʾayo Sayṭān la-Herods qāla ba-qāl (6938) / በእንተ፡ ዘከመ፡ አስተርአየቶ፡ ለቴዎፍሎስ፡… እምድካመ፡ ፍኖት፡… ወእንዘ፡ ከመዝ፡ አስተርአዮ፡ ሰይጣን፡ ለሄሮድስ፡ ቃለ፡ በቃል፡.


MAC0003.

MSS: G-3; VLVE 298(131r).
EMML: 6938 (18r); 2059 (127v); 2060 (166v); 7543 (12r); 2056 (132v); 2058 (21r); 1581 (47v).

MAC0004.
Title: Deacon Michael, the grocer and the ring that was found in the fish.
Text:
PEth: 41.74 (101v-104r);
EMIP: 601.60 (35v–37r);
MSS: G-4; ZBNE 62-51; VLVE 298 (45r); CBS-53; DULE 12 (40v).
EMML: 2275 (191v); 6938 (20r); 1960 (3r, 6r); 5520 (27v); 1946 (97r); 2378 (18v); 2059 (109v); 2060 (12v); 2066 (29v); 2802 (19v); 7543 (13r).
Keywords: Deacons; Fish; Grocers; Michael, deacon; Rings; Semahu;
Incipit: Wa-hallo ʾaḥadu bǝʾǝsi ba-hagar za-Sāmu, diyāqon wǝʾǝtu za-sǝmu Mikāʾel, wa-yāfaqqǝrā la-ʾƎgzǝʾǝtǝna… bǝzuḫa wa-yǝtlaʾakkā ba-kwǝllu ḫaylu, ʿaṭṭār za-wǝʾǝtu śayyāṭe ʾǝm-kwǝllu mabālǝʿt (2058) / ወሀሎ፡ አሐዱ፡ ብእሲ፡ በሀገር፡ ዘሳሙ፡ ዲያቆን፡ ውእቱ፡ ዘስሙ፡ ሚካኤል፡ ወያፈቅራ፡ ለእግዝእትነ፡… ብዙኀ፡ ወይትለአካ፡ በኵሉ፡ ኀይሉ፡ ዐጣር፡ ዘውእቱ፡ ሠያጤ፡ እምኵሉ፡ መባልዕት፡.


MAC0005.
Title: The Frenchman whose wife was unable to have children.
Text: Cerulli, Il libro, p. 360.
PEth:
MSS: G-5; CRA 53-31; VLVE 272 (223v); 298 (46v); CBS-54.
EMML: 6938 (23r); 2059 (93v); 2060 (119v); 7543(14v); 2056 (49r); 2058 (23v); 2999 (168r).
Keywords: Childlessness; Children; Europeans [Afrengi]; Frenchmen; France; Healings, Childlessness; Wives;
Incipit: Wa-hallo ʾaḥadu bǝʾǝsi ba-hagara ʾAfrǝngi ʾǝm-ʾadyāma ʾAfrānsā za-yāfaqqǝrā la-ʾƎgzǝʾǝtǝna… ʾǝm-nǝʾsu wa-yǝtlaʾakkā ba-kwǝllu ḫaylu. Wa-soba baṣḥa ʾamṭāna ʾawsǝbo, ʾastawāsabǝwwo ʾabawihu walatta ʾǝm-awlāda ʾAfrǝngi (6938) / ወሀሎ፡ አሐዱ፡ ብእሲ፡ በሀገረ፡ አፍርንጊ፡ እምአድያመ፡ አፍራንሳ፡ ዘያፈቅራ፡ ለእግዝእትነ፡… እምንእሱ፡ ወይትለአካ፡ በኵሉ፡ ኀይሉ። ወሶበ፡ በጽሐ፡ አምጣነ፡ አውስቦ፡ አስተዋሰብዎ፡ አበዊሁ፡ ወለተ፡ እምአውላደ፡ አፍርንጊ፡.


MAC0006.
Title: During the famine of 1120 MM [likely 1404 CE], the Arabs try to plunder the monasteries of Egypt.
Text:
Summary: Cerulli, Il libro, p. 174.
PEth:
MSS: G-6; VLVE 298 (49v); CBS-55.
EMML: 6938(27v); 5520(130v); 2059(40r); 2066 (92r); 2802 (115v); 7543 (16v); 3051 (73r).
Keywords: Egypt; Famines; Martyrs dates; Matthew I, Patriarch of Alexandria; Mesr; Monasteries; Preservation from plundering; Robbers;
Incipit: Wa-kona ba-1000 wa-100 wa-20 ʿāmata Samāʿtāt nǝṣuḥān, ba-mawāʿǝlihu la-ʾab ʾǝgziʾ liqa ṗāṗṗāsāt ʾAbbā Mātewos, wa-kona ba-hagara Mǝsr raḥāb ʿabiyy (6938) / ወኮነ፡ በ፲፻ወ፻ወ፳ዓመተ፡ ሰማዕታት፡ ንጹሓን፡ በመዋዕሊሁ፡ ለአብ፡ እግዚእ፡ ሊቀ፡ ጳጳሳት፡ አባ፡ ማቴዎስ፡ ወኮነ፡ በሀገረ፡ ምስር፡ ረሓብ፡ ዐቢይ።.


MAC0007.
Title: The monk of Däbrä Qaləmon who did not fast.
Text: Budge, Miracles, p. 42.
English translation: Budge, One Hundred, p. 87.
Summary: Cerulli, Il libro, p. 166.
PEth: 20.78 (81v-82r); 41.75 (104r-106r); 46.28 (28r-29v); 46.67 (74v-77r); 47.28 (85r-86v);
EMIP: 601.28 (20r–21r);
MSS: G-7; ZBNE 60-29; 61-27; CRA 52-35; CRA 54 (91r); CRA 55 (91r); SBLE 32-28; BM 2-31; 3-36; VLVE 267 (56v); 298 (23r, 50v); SALE 23-27; 43-29; LUE 30-40; 32-28; CBS-28; CCBE 951-28; AECE 1 (30r).
EMML: 2275 (194r); 6938 (29v); 5520 (31v); 2378 (20v); 6640 (49r); 2060 (195r); 2066 (31v, 135v); 2802 (22v); 6196 (81r); 7543 (17v).
Keywords: Däbrä Qaləmon; Fasting; Hail Mary; Icons; Monasteries; Monks;
Incipit: Wa-hallo ba-Däbrä qǝddus ʿabiyy ʾAbbā Sāmuʾel za-Qaləmon beta krǝstiyān śannāyt ba-sǝma ʾƎgzǝʾǝtǝna… wa-kona wǝsta zātti beta krǝstiyān sǝʿl ʿabiyy wa-mankǝr / ወሀሎ፡ በደብረ፡ ቅዱስ፡ ዐቢይ፡ አባ፡ ሳሙኤል፡ ዘቀልሞን፡ ቤተ፡ ክርስቲያን፡ ሠናይት፡ በስመ፡ እግዝእትነ፡… ወኮነ፡ ውስተ፡ ዛቲ፡ ቤተ፡ ክርስቲያን፡ ስዕል፡ ዐቢይ፡ ወመንክር፡ (6938).
Wa-hallo ʾaḥadu bǝʾǝsi manakos ba-Däbrä ʾAbbā Sāmuʾel za-Qaləmon wa-yāfaqqǝrā la-ʾƎgzǝʾǝtǝna Maryam wa-yānabbǝb watra taʾammeḫota malʾak lelita wa-maʿalta. Wa-zǝntussa bǝʾǝsi ʾiyyeṣawwǝm wa-ʾiyyǝṣelli wa-yǝtmessal kama ʾabd wa-ʾǝnbuz / ወሀሎ፡ አሐዱ፡ ብእሲ፡ መነኮስ፡ በደብረ፡ አባ፡ ሳሙኤል፡ ዘቀልሞን፡ ወያፈቅራ፡ ለእግዝእትነ፡ ማርያም፡ ወያነብብ፡ ወትረ፡ ተአምኆተ፡ መልአክ፡ ሌሊተ፡ ወመዐልተ። ወዝንቱሰ፡ ብእሲ፡ ኢይጸውም፡ ወኢይጼሊ፡ ወይትሜሰል፡ ከመ፡ አብድ፡ ወእንቡዝ፡ (2378).


MAC0008.
Title: The monks of Däbrä Qaləmon who were despoiled by Berbers.
PEth: 41.82 (115v-118r): How the Virgin Mary saved the monks of Däbrä Qälmon from Arabs; 46.66 (72v-74v): How the Virgin Mary saved the monks from the hand of Muslims in the monastery of Qäləmen;
MSS: G-8; VLVE 298 (52v); CBS-56.
EMML: 6938 (32r); 2060 (18v); 7543 (18v); 2056 (135v); 3051 (74r); 2058 (28v); 3031 (89v).
Keywords: Abbots; Berbers; Däbrä Qaləmon; Monasteries; Monks; Robbers;
Incipit: Wa-kona ba-ʾaḥadu ʾǝm-mawāʿǝl, ḥoru sabʾ manakosāt ʾǝm-Däbrä ʾAbbā Sāmuʾel za-Qaləmon la-faṣṣǝmo mafqǝda dabr / ወኮነ፡ በአሐዱ፡ እመዋዕል፡ ሖሩ፡ ሰብእ፡ መነኮሳት፡ እምደብረ፡ አባ፡ ሳሙኤል፡ ቀልሞን፡ ለፈጽሞ፡ መፍቅደ፡ ደብር፡ (6938).
